noun. 必需品</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">necessary adj. 必须的</strong></p><p style="white-space: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We were discussing <span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;">the <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">necessity</span></em></strong> of</span> employing more staff. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们在讨论<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">是否需要</strong>雇用更多员工。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">4. 词链儿：best effort 最大努力、尽力</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Please <span style="text-decoration: underline;">exert your <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">best efforts</span></em></strong> to</span> settle the matter.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>请尽<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">最大努力</strong>解决此事。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Success is primarily determined by making right choices, secondarily by <span style="text-decoration: underline;">making <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">best</span></em></strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"> effort</span></em></strong>.</span> <br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>成功的首要因素是选择；<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">奋斗</strong>是第二位的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>You've always got to<span style="text-decoration: underline;"> put in your very <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">best effort</span></em></strong>.</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你总是要付出<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">最大的努力</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>I didn't really try, so it wasn't my <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">best effort</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我并没有真正去尝试，所以这并不是我<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">最大的努力</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Give your <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">best effort</span></em></strong>, because <span style="text-decoration: underline;">you are worth your <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">best effort</span></em></strong>.</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">付出你<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">最大的努力</strong>，因为你值得付出<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">最大的努力</strong>。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img class="rich_pages wxw-img" data-ratio="0.4705882" For me, I don't like it. </em></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img class="rich_pages wxw-img" data-ratio="0.6676876" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKeVKNpxN3S2C77FN4rKnx3vhqribEPwm9COUHRf7l4WATXeZoJBkgVG4K0taK6uTXXvjZCYypiamENQ/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="653" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">But here we have a lot of people who come to the island, who are from the middle east. It’s very, very hot all the time. So they will come to Langkawi and Malaysia in the rainy seasons because they never get rain in their countries. So I think it’s funny if I’m driving around and I’m like, oh, no, it’s raining. It’s gonna get hard. I see them and they're walking around on the streets going like, yeah! Rain! seen snow before. I lived in Australia…I mean in Australia, it sometimes snows high up in the mountain. But when I lived there, there has never snowed. I've never seen snow. And then I lived in Europe for a while, that was in south of Europe. So it never snow there and I also lived in southeast Asia for a long time, and it also never snows here because it's all tropical. So I’d never seen snow and I have tell some of my friends that. And I have a lot of, I’d say in the school that I used to work at, we had a lot of American teachers as well. And they lived in places where it would snow for months and months in the year. And I say, no, I’ve never seen snow. That was amazing. And they’re like what? You’ve never seen snow? And I get all excited about it. And then they say, no, it’s not as exciting as you think. It’s not that much fun.  But it would be! So talking back about the customers, how long would they usually stay in the hotel in that place?</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">They usually stay between two and four days, I would say. </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgba(94, 169, 210, 0.6);padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">program</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ ˈprəʊɡræm  /</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> n. 程序；计划；大纲</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vt. 用程序指令；为…制订计划；为…安排节目</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vi. 编程序；安排节目；设计电脑程式</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> the university's graduate programs 大学研究生课程</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> a TV program 电视节目</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">explore</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ ɪkˈsplɔː(r)/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vt. 探测；探索；探险</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vi. 探测；探险；探索</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">companies exploring for (= searching for)oil 石油勘探公司</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">That's the first subject we're exploring today.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这是我们今天要探讨的第一个话题。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We want to go further to explore.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们想进一步探索。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">idiom </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ ˈɪdɪəm / n. 成语，习语；土话</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Some English idioms often baffle English learners.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有些英语成语经常使英语学习者感到困惑。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">‘Let the cat out of the bag’ is an idiom meaning to tell a secret by mistake. “让猫从袋子里跑出来”是惯用语，意思是无意中泄露秘密。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">deep</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/di:p/ adj. 位于深处的, 纵深的,深色的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">depth /depθ/n. 深, 深度, 纵深</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">extraordinary </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ɪkˈstrɔːrdəneri/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> adj. 非常奇怪的,非同寻常的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It's a really extraordinary period of human history.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这真的是人类历史上的非凡时刻。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">cook </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ kʊk/ v. 做饭，烹调；伪造；n. 厨师</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The cook is looking at a cookbook to cook us something good.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">厨师正在看菜谱，找美味的食物。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">board</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/bɔ:d/n. 板, 牌子,纸板, 木板,委员会</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Night fell. A profound silence reigned on board.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">夜幕降临。船上笼罩着深深的寂静。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The application was endorsed by the governers' board.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">申请书已由董事会批准。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">represent </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ ˌreprɪˈzent /</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vt. 表现, 描绘,代表, 象征, 表示,作为…的代表</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It represents a wish for an annual surplus.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这不是年年有余吗。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">On the map, blue represents water and brown represents land.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">在地图上，蓝色代表海，棕色代表陆地。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">advertising campaign广告活动</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">advertising</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/'ædvərtaɪzɪŋ/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 广告, 广告宣传</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj. 广告的；广告业的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> A good advertising campaignwill increase our sales. 良好的广告宣传活动会增加我们的销售量。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> Cigarette advertising has been banned. 香烟广告已遭禁止。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">campaign  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/kæmˈpeɪn/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vi. 作战；参加活动；参加竞选</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 战役；运动；活动</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">an anti-smoking campaign 反对吸烟的运动</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">But campaign season is in full swing.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">但竞选活动正在如火如荼地进行。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">usefulness and versatility 实用性和多功能性 </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">use n.使用，用途；vt.利用</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">useful adj.有用的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">usefulness </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ ˈjuːsfəlnəs/n. 有用,有益,有效</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The building has outlived its usefulness. 这座楼房已超过使用年限了。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">versatility /ˌvɜːsəˈtɪləti/ </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 多才多艺,多用途,多功能,活动性,反复无常</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Incredible </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ ɪnˈkredəbl /</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj. 不能相信的, 不可信的,难以置信的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">So bamboo is a pretty incredible material.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">竹子是一种令人难以置信的材料。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">edible </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ ˈedəbl/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj. 可食用的 n. 食物；食品</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">This apple is rotten and no longer edible.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这个苹果是腐烂的，不能食用。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The cake was garnished with edible decorations.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">蛋糕上装饰着可食用的装饰品。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.没有听出来的意群：可能包括连读或者省音,分析错误的原因并做笔记。</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.没有听出来或听错的单词:每篇校对后写在听写笔记下面并罗列,这些才是你每天的进步之基。</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(188, 132, 37);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">今日听写答案</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;color: rgba(122, 120, 124, 0.91);font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">（请务必听写后校对） </span></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">红色连读</span><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">；<span style="color: rgba(46, 159, 238, 0.863);box-sizing: border-box;">蓝色爆破省读</span>；<span style="color: rgb(255, 129, 36);box-sizing: border-box;">橙色弱读</span></span></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;border-width: 1px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(206, 169, 203);padding: 10px;box-shadow: rgb(204, 204, 204) 2.6px 2.6px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 17px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;">Monday</span><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">On this program, we explore commo<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">n e</span></span>xpressions and idioms a little more in depth.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">本集中，我们将更深入地探讨一些常见的表达和习语。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Today, we discuss a popular and common food – eggs!</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">今天，我们将讨论一种很常见的比较受欢迎的食物</span><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">——</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">鸡蛋！</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">People who like eggs think they are egg-xecllent (excellent)! Egg-traordinary (extraordinary)!! Egg-mazing (amazing)!!!</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">喜欢吃鸡蛋的人认为他们是</span><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">“egg-xecllent (excellent)(</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">优秀</span><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">)! Egg-traordinary (extraordinary)(</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">非常优秀</span><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">)!! Egg-mazing (amazing)(</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">优秀到爆</span><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">)!!!”</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Okay, tha<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 112, 192);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> las<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t o</span></span>ne didn'<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 112, 192);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> really work.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">好吧，最后一个不太好用。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">So, let's tal<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">k a</span></span>bout cooking with eggs.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">所以，我们来谈谈</span><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">“</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">烹饪鸡蛋</span><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">”</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">In the mid-1970s, the U.S. American Egg Board -- a group tha<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 112, 192);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> represents egg farmers -- wante<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 112, 192);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> to create an advertising campaign tha<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 112, 192);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> captured the usefulness and versatility of the egg.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">20</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">世纪</span><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">70</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">年代中期，美国鸡蛋委员会</span><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">——</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">一个代表蛋农的组织</span><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">——</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">想要发起一场广告活动，捕捉鸡蛋的用途和多功能性。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Its ad campaign, called "Th<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">e I</span></span>ncredible, Edible Egg," tol<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d o</span></span>f all the health benefits and showed all the ways we can use eggs in our meals.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">该公司的广告活动名为</span><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">“</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">不可思议的可食用鸡蛋</span><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">”</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">，讲述了鸡蛋对健康的所有好处，并展示了我们在膳食中使用鸡蛋的所有方式。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">All day Fledge flew steadily with untiring wings; eastward with the river to guide him, through the mountains and over the wild wooded hills, and then over the great waterfall and down, and down, to where the woods of Narnia were darkened by the shadow of the mighty cliff, till at last, when the sky was growing red with sunset behind them, he saw a place where many creatures were gathered together by the riverside. And soon he could see Aslan himself in the midst of them. Fledge glided down, spread out his four legs, closed his wings, and landed cantering. Then he pulled up. The children dismounted. Digory saw all the animals, dwarfs, satyrs, nymphs, and other things drawing back to the left and right to make way for him.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">一整天，弗兰奇都不知疲倦地扇动着翅膀，稳稳地飞行。越过高山，飞过森林覆盖的原始山区，过了大瀑布，高度越来越低，一直飞到在高大岩壁投下的阴影中显得灰暗无光的纳尼亚林区。最后，背后的天空被夕阳染得绯红。它看见河边聚集了许多动物，很快就看见阿斯兰也在其中。弗兰奇收了双翅，伸开四蹄滑了下来，慢跑着落在地上。停稳后，孩子们下了马，迪格雷看见所有的动物、小矮人、森林之神、河泽仙女等全都朝两边退去，为他留出一条路来。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：你要喝点什么吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：我想来点喝的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：我有水、果汁、冰茶还是你想要更烈的吗?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：更烈的会很好。你有酒吗?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：我有。你会喜欢红葡萄酒还是白葡萄酒?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：我喜欢白的,但那要看你都有什么样的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：我有霞多丽。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：那太好了。我要一杯。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：太好了!我应该也拿来了一些奶酪和饼干。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：那会和白酒很搭配。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：太好了！等我去厨房把它们取来。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：你真是个极好的主人。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Can I get you something to drink?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: I would love something to drink.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: I have water, juice, ice tea or did you want something stronger?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Something stronger would be great. Do you have wine?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: I do. Would you prefer red wine or white wine?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: I'd love white, but it depends what kind you have.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: I have Chardonnay.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: That would be great. I'll take a glass.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Excellent! Should I also bring out some cheese and crackers.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: That would go so well with the wine.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Great! Just give me a moment to get that from the kitchen.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: You are such a wonderful host.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I hate to cut and run, but I have a meeting in 15 minutes.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我真不愿意这么____________，但是我15分钟后有一个会议。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">匆忙地离开</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">汉译英</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">夜空，是人类与生俱来的共享资源。原则上来说，任何人、在任何地方，都可以欣赏夜空的美，你只需轻轻抬头仰望。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">然而，如同我们身边很多其它美丽的事物一样，夜空正在逐渐消逝，而我们却未曾察觉，因为，我们根本看都没看一眼。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The sky is inherently democratic. It's accessible, in principle, anyway, by anyone, everywhere, just simply by the act of looking up.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">But like so many beautiful things around us, it's slipping away from us, and we haven't even noticed, because we're honestly not really looking.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><p style="text-align: center;outline: 0px;max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: 0.544px;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;"><strong style="outline: 0px;max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: 0.544px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="font-family:-apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, Helvetica Neue, PingFang SC, Hiragino Sans GB, Microsoft YaHei UI, Microsoft YaHei, Arial, sans-serif;">11.8 每日一句：</span></strong><strong style="outline: 0px;max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: 0.544px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="font-family:-apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, Helvetica Neue, PingFang SC, Hiragino Sans GB, Microsoft YaHei UI, Microsoft YaHei, Arial, sans-serif;">What are you doing here?   </span></strong></p><p style="text-align: center;outline: 0px;max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: 0.544px;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;"><strong style="outline: 0px;max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: 0.544px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="outline: 0px;max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: 0.544px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="font-family:-apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, YaHei, Arial, sans-serif;"></span></strong><strong style="outline: 0px;max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: 0.544px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="font-family:-apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, Helvetica Neue, PingFang SC, Hiragino Sans GB, Microsoft YaHei UI, Microsoft YaHei, Arial, sans-serif;"></span></strong></p><section style="box-sizing: border-box;font-style: normal;text-align: justify;font-size: 16px;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-weight: 400;text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img class="rich_pages wxw-img" data-ratio="0.42" 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">今日发音练习重点：</strong></p><ol class="list-paddingleft-2" style="list-style-type: decimal;"><li style="font-size: 14px;font-weight: bold;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(18, 17, 17);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong><span style="font-size: 14px;">while/I'll 包含的/<span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;text-align: start;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">aɪl/为难发音组；</span></span></strong></p></section></li><li style="font-size: 14px;font-weight: bold;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(18, 17, 17);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong><span style="font-size: 14px;">意群停顿：so much has changed / since you've been away//。</span></strong><br/></p></section></li></ol></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-weight: 400;transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);text-align: left;margin: 20px 0% 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 40%;border-width: 0px 6px 0px 0px;border-style: solid;border-left-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);border-right-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);padding: 0px;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;background-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(252, 252, 252);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">言之有物</em></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-weight: 400;text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. 词链儿：stay a while 久留</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It's only 11:00, <em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">stay a while</span></strong></em>.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>才11点啊，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">再待会嘛</strong>！</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He doesn't live here: he is only <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">staying a while</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他不住在这儿，只不过<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">暂时呆一下</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. 词链儿：put XX to rights 整顿XX，以使其恢复正常</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">此处right为名词，本短语中right应为复数形式。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He helped his mother <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">put </span></em></strong><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(18, 17, 17);box-sizing: border-box;">things</span></span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"> to rights</span></em></strong> after his father died.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他父亲死后，他帮助妈妈<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">使</strong>一切<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">恢复如初</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">This medicine will soon <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">put</span></em></strong> you <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">to rights</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这药可以<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">使</strong>你很快<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">康复</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">If you wanted to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">put</span></em></strong> the world <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">to rights</span></em></strong>, who should you begin with: yourself or others?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">如果你想<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">让</strong>世界<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">恢复正常</strong>，你应该从谁开始:你自己还是别人?</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-weight: 400;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">3. 建议背诵整句：</strong></p><p style="font-weight: 400;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">So much has changed since you've been away.</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong>你离开以后，发生了好多变化。</strong></p><p style="font-weight: 400;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="font-weight: 400;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">① 词链儿：so much has changed since.... 自从...以来很多事都改变了。</strong></p><p style="font-weight: 400;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="font-weight: 400;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">So much has changed since</span></em></strong> the pandemic first began.</p><p style="font-weight: 400;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">疫情<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">以来发生了很多改变</strong>。</p><p style="font-weight: 400;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="font-weight: 400;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">Not much has changed since</span></em></strong> he left.</p><p style="font-weight: 400;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他离开后，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">没发生什么改变</strong>。</p><p style="font-weight: 400;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="font-weight: 400;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">So much has changed since</span></em></strong> the last election.</p><p style="font-weight: 400;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">自</strong>上次选举<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">以来</strong>，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">发生了很多变化</strong>。</p><p style="font-weight: 400;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="font-weight: 400;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">So much has changed since</span></em></strong> I was in high school.</p><p style="font-weight: 400;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">自从</strong>我上高中<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">以来</strong>，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">发生了很大的变化</strong>。</p><p style="font-weight: 400;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="font-weight: 400;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">② 词链儿：be away 离开 </strong></p><p style="font-weight: 400;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">此处指“逝去”，等同于pass away</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-weight: 400;transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);text-align: left;margin: 20px 0% 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 40%;border-width: 0px 6px 0px 0px;border-style: solid;border-left-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);border-right-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);padding: 0px;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;background-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(252, 252, 252);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 1px;padding: 0px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(250, 224, 74);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"># </strong></span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">地道表达：Quiet coyote</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">coyote n.〔北美西部和墨西哥的〕丛林狼，郊狼</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Quiet Coyote意思是：“嘘……大家安静！”当你希望让一群叽叽喳喳说话的人变得安静下来，就可以说：Quiet Coyote。</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Quiet Coyote通常用于老师对低年级学生们讲话时的情景，而且往往说的时候还会配合一个手势——大拇指、中指和无名指捏在一起，食指和小指朝上竖起，整个手形成一匹狼的样子，这个手势就可爱。</p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 80%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 2px;border-width: 1px;border-radius: 4px;border-style: dashed;border-color: rgba(157, 187, 254, 0.46);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;height: auto;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 2px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKdk18ib2kjuE3s56ycLz5Kt8sjaUwqZ89LFhoc6EfNZgia68t3sjxesvtD6VzRoJNgNEonc7JUyYd3A/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="604" style="vertical-align: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;">Quiet coyote is a hand signal which is often used by teachers and parents as a non-verbal sign to instruct children to stop speaking and listen.</span></em><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;">To use it, you simply make your hand into the shape of a coyote with a closed mouth and pricked-up ears.</span></em></span></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: 160);box-sizing: border-box;">Featured in the Disney movie Soul, the quiet coyote signal can be a very effective method of silencing a large group of children in a positive and empowering border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img class="rich_pages wxw-img" data-ratio="0.4898148" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/L4LJPfaSIKdk18ib2kjuE3s56ycLz5Kt8zJpLLibNdYWIKXuAVqkfavo9j8p0TJWHszjTwe9P0bQaibEEOjU74d3g/640?wx_fmt=png" data-type="png" data-w="1080" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 1px;padding: 0px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(250, 224, 74);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"># </strong></span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">地道表达：aloof</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">aloof /əˈluːf/ 其实是来自航海术语，由a-（去，往）+loof（朝向上风方向）这两部分构成，意思就是“朝向上风方向驶去”。</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">由于船头朝向上风是为了避开下风方向的障碍物，因此aloof又衍生出“躲避的、远离的”这层含义，并进一步衍生出“<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">疏远的、冷漠的</strong>”等比喻意。现在，人们几乎只使用aloof的比喻之意，而不再使用它的本意。如在街上看到摔倒的老人时，有些人的做法就是保持aloof。 </p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She had always kept herself <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">aloof</span> from the boys in class.</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她对班上的男生一直很<em style="box-sizing: style="font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 1px;padding: 0px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(250, 224, 74);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"># </strong></span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">地道表达：Quiet coyote</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">coyote n.〔北美西部和墨西哥的〕丛林狼，郊狼</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Quiet Coyote意思是：“嘘……大家安静！”当你希望让一群叽叽喳喳说话的人变得安静下来，就可以说：Quiet Coyote。</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Quiet Coyote通常用于老师对低年级学生们讲话时的情景，而且往往说的时候还会配合一个手势——大拇指、中指和无名指捏在一起，食指和小指朝上竖起，整个手形成一匹狼的样子，这个手势就可爱。</p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 80%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 2px;border-width: 1px;border-radius: 4px;border-style: dashed;border-color: rgba(157, 187, 254, 0.46);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;height: auto;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 2px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><img class="rich_pages wxw-img" data-ratio="0.7466887" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKdk18ib2kjuE3s56ycLz5Kt8sjaUwqZ89LFhoc6EfNZgia68t3sjxesvtD6VzRoJNgNEonc7JUyYd3A/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="604" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;" width="100%"/></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 1px;padding: 0px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;">Quiet coyote is a hand signal which is often used by teachers and parents as a non-verbal sign to instruct children to stop speaking and listen.</span></em><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;">To use it, you simply make your hand into the shape of a coyote with a closed mouth and pricked-up ears.</span></em></span></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;">Featured in the Disney movie Soul, the quiet coyote signal can be a very effective method of silencing a large group of children in a positive and empowering way.</span></em></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img class="rich_pages wxw-img" data-ratio="0.4898148" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/L4LJPfaSIKdk18ib2kjuE3s56ycLz5Kt8zJpLLibNdYWIKXuAVqkfavo9j8p0TJWHszjTwe9P0bQaibEEOjU74d3g/640?wx_fmt=png" data-type="png" data-w="1080" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 1px;padding: 0px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(250, 224, 74);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"># </strong></span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">地道表达：aloof</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">aloof /əˈluːf/ 其实是来自航海术语，由a-（去，往）+loof（朝向上风方向）这两部分构成，意思就是“朝向上风方向驶去”。</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">由于船头朝向上风是为了避开下风方向的障碍物，因此aloof又衍生出“躲避的、远离的”这层含义，并进一步衍生出“<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">疏远的、冷漠的</strong>”等比喻意。现在，人们几乎只使用aloof的比喻之意，而不再使用它的本意。如在街上看到摔倒的老人时，有些人的做法就是保持aloof。 </p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She had always kept herself <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">aloof</span> from the boys in class.</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她对班上的男生一直很<em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">冷漠</span></em>。</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She seemed rather <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">aloof</span> when in fact she was just shy.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她看似<em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">孤傲不</span></em><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">群</span></em>，可实际上只是腼腆。</p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She felt exhausted after<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"> the traumas of</span> recent weeks. </p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她经受了最近几个星期的<em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">痛苦</span></em>之后感到精疲力竭。</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">the trauma of </span>marriage breakdown</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">婚姻破裂带来的<em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">心理创伤</span></em></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">get over/recover from<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"> trauma</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">从<em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: 114);border-bottom-right-radius: 0px;padding: 0px 5px 4px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词汇补充</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgba(94, 169, 210, 0.6);padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">mousse  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/muːs/ </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a sweet food made from a mixture of cream, eggs, and fruit or chocolate, which is eaten when it is cold n.奶油冻；慕斯；慕丝</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">pack </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/pæk/ </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">to put something into a box or other container, so that it can be moved, sold, or storedpack something in/into something v.包装；打包；n.纸盒</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">omelet (also omelet American English) </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ˈɒmlət $ ˈɑːm-/ </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">eggs mixed together and cooked in hot fat, sometimes with other foods added n.鸡蛋卷</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">gang </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ɡæŋ/ </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a group of young people who spend time together, and who are often involved in crime or drugs and who often fight against other groups n.一群；一帮；一伙</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Merengue </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/mə'reŋɡeɪ/ n.梅伦格舞；梅伦格舞曲</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">elegant </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ˈeləɡənt/ </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">beautiful, attractive, or graceful adj.优美的；雅致的；讲究的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a tall, elegant young woman.一位身材高挑、举止优雅的年轻女子。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">an idea or a plan that is elegant is very intelligent yet simple adj.巧妙的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">an elegant solution to the problem.这个问题的巧妙解决方案.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">incredible </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ɪnˈkredəbəl/ </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">extremely good, large, or great  adj.极好的；极大的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The view is just incredible.这里的景色极佳。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">too strange to be believed, or very difficult to believe adj.不能相信的；难以置信的；</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It’s incredible how much Tom has changed since he met Sally.Tom和Sally相遇后，变化之大令人难以置信。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">edible </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ˈedəbəl/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">something that is edible can be eaten adj.可食用的；可以吃的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Dish </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/dɪʃ/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a flat container with low sides, for serving food from or cooking food in n.菜；盘子</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a type of food that is cooked in a particular way and served as part of a meal n.菜肴</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The menu includes a wide selection of vegetarian dishes.菜单上有各种各样的素菜可供选择。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Sunny-side up </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">an egg that is cooked sunny-side up is cooked in hot fat on one side only, and not turned over in the pan n.单煎一面蛋黄在上的煎鸡蛋</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">scramble </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ˈskræmbəl/  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">to climb up, down, or over something quickly and with difficulty, especially using your hands to help you v.爬</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">They tried to scramble up the cliff.他们试图爬上悬崖。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">to struggle or compete with other people to get or reach something v.争取；争先恐后</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Thousands of people will be scrambling for tickets.数以千计的人将会争先恐后地抢票。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">scramble an egg </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">to cook an egg by mixing the white and yellow parts together and heating it in a pan 炒鸡蛋</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">poach </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/pəʊtʃ $ poʊtʃ/ </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">to cook an egg in or over gently boiling water, without its shell v.水煮(荷包蛋)</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">poached eggs 水煮蛋</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">fried  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/fraɪd/  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">having been cooked in hot oil v.用油煎</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">fried chicken炸鸡</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">idiom </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ˈɪdiəm/ </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a group of words that has a special meaning that is different from the ordinary meaning of each separate word. For example, ‘under the weather’ is an idiom meaning ‘ill’. n.成语；习语；惯用语</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">这让我们想到了一个与烹饪相关的习语：</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, border-box;">有失才有得</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">)”</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">We often say thi</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s a</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">s an answer to several different situations.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">我们经常用这句话来回答不同的情况。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">Here's one:Let's say you have an important goal or task.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">比如：假设你有一个重要的目标或任务。</span></p><p style="text-align: powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The children now noticed these two for the first time. They were dressed in strange and beautiful clothes, and from their shoulders rich robes flowed out behind them to where four dwarfs held up the King's train and four river nymphs the Queen's. Their heads were bare; but Helen had let her hair down and it made a great improvement in her appearance. But it was neither hair nor clothes that made them look so different from their old selves. Their faces had a new expression, especially the King's. All the sharpness and cunning and quarrelsomeness which he had picked up as a London cabby seemed to have been washed away, and the courage and kindness which he had always had were easier to see. Perhaps it was the air of the young world that had done it, or talking with Aslan, or both.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">孩子们现在才注意到这一对夫妻。他们穿着奇特而美丽的衣服，华贵的长袍从肩上一直拖到地上，四个小矮人托起国王的袍裾，四个河泽仙女托起王后的裙裾。他们的头上没有装饰，但海伦把头发披了下来，显得更加动人。然而，不是头发也不是服装使他们与过去迥然不同，而是脸上有了一种崭新的表情，尤其是国王。他在伦敦当马车夫时养成的尖刻、狡诈和好争吵的秉性全部涤荡一空，勇敢和善良的本性则比较明显。也许，是这个年轻世界的空气或与阿斯兰的谈话产生了这样的效果，也许两者兼有。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：很久没见你了！</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：我知道。你一点也没变。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：哦，别说谎。我有点胖了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：我们都有点胖了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：告诉我孩子们都还好吗。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：他们都很好，你的呢？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：他们很好，长得很快。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：你还在做原来的工作还是在做一些别的工作？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：没有。我三年前离开了那，开始我自己的生意。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：祝贺你！你一直都有独立精神。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：谢谢。目前为止一切进展顺利。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：喝完咖啡我想了解更多关于你的事情。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: It's been so long since I've seen you!</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: I know. You haven't changed a bit.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Oh, stop lying. I've gained a little weight.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: We all have gained some weight.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Tell me how the kids are doing.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: They are doing well, and yours?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: They are doing so well, growing up so fast.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Are you at the same job or are you doing something else?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: No. I left that place three years ago to start my own business.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Congratulations! You always had an independent spirit.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Thanks. It's going really well so far.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: I'd love to hear more about it over a cup of coffee.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">After much scheming and lobbying, he got the upper hand over his opponent.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他费了不少心机，四处争取支持，终于_____________。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">占了对手的上风</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">汉译英</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">那我们看的究竟是什么呢？我们在看手机、玩电脑，我们注视着各种各样的电子屏幕。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">说实在的，我们甚至很少费心去抬头注视彼此，更不要说走出房门、抬头仰望真正的天空了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">越来越多的人认为，夜空的消逝是科技进步、社会发展的必然结果。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">So what do we look at instead? Well, we look at our phones, we look at our computers, we look at screens of all kinds.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">And honestly, we rarely even take the trouble to look up enough to see each other, let alone taking that next step to looking up at the actual sky.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Now, there's a tendency to think that the loss of our dark night skies is the inevitable outcome of progress, change, technology.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><p style="text-align: center;outline: 0px;max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: 0.544px;white-space: normal;background-color: 为后鼻音+元音连读；</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. scared /skeəd $ skerd/ 控制元音发音的开口度。</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px,
