0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. risk</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">① 动词：冒…的风险；冒险做XX</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">risk XX/doing XX</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He <em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">risked</span></strong></em> his life to save her.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">冒着</strong>生命<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">危险</strong>去救她。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It was a difficult decision but we decided to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">risk</span></em></strong> it.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这件事决心难下，但我们决定<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">冒险</strong>一试。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>But I would <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">risk</span></em></strong> messing up that perfect room every day just to see that book.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">但我<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">冒着</strong>每天把那个完美房间搞得一团糟的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">风险</strong>，就为了看那本书。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>But little girls should not have to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">risk</span></em></strong> their life for this.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">但小女孩不应该为此<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">冒</strong>生命<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">危险</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">risk </span></em></strong>destroying in a single day all the …</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你这么做会在一天内将我们长期…</p></section><section border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">take risks</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">take chances</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: risks</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">投资就是要<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">冒风险</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. 词链儿：there is no point (in) doing XX</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">做XX是无用的</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">= there's no use (in) doing XX</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">= there is no purpose in doing XX</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">现在抱怨已完全<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">没有用了</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p 39);box-sizing: border-box;">There's no point</span></em></strong> <span style="text-decoration: underline;">getting upset about</span> it. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">犯不着</strong>为此事难过。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">当大家都在这里奋斗的时候我可完全<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">没必要</strong>把自己拴在办公桌前。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词汇补充</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;box-sizing: rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">请上下滑动查看</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: transparent;padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(17, 1, 1);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.in order to do sth. 目的是；以便；为了</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英英释义：with the purpose or intention of doing or achieving sth</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She arrived early in order to get a good seat. 她早早到场，好找个好位置。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.omelet  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英[ˈɒmlɪi] 美[ˈɑmlət]</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 煎蛋卷；炒鸡蛋</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英英释义：beaten eggs or an egg mixture cooked until just set,may be folded around e.g. ham or cheese or jelly</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Let's make sure we get a pretty good omelet out of it.让我们用它来做出美味的蛋卷吧。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">3.idiom  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ ˈɪdiəm  ; NAmE ˈɪdiəm  /</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n.习语；成语；惯用语</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英英释义：a group of words whose meaning is different from the meanings of the individual words</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">‘Let the cat out of the bag’ is an idiom meaning to tell a secret by mistake. “让猫从袋子里跑出来”是惯用语，意思是无意中泄露秘密。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">4.mess  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ mes  ; NAmE mes  /</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n.肮脏；杂乱；不整洁</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英英释义：a dirty or untidy state</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">My hair's a real mess! 我的头发太乱了。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The room was in a mess. 这个房间杂乱不堪。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">5.cardboard  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ ˈkɑːdbɔːd  ; NAmE ˈkɑːrdbɔːrd  /</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n.硬纸板，卡纸板（常用于制造盒子）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英英释义：stiff material like very thick paper, often used for making boxes</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a piece of cardboard 一张硬纸板</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">6.paint  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ peɪnt  ; NAmE peɪnt  / </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n.油漆；油漆涂层</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英英释义：a liquid that is put on surfaces to give them a particular colour; a layer of this liquid when it has dried on a surface</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The woodwork has recently been given a fresh coat of paint. 木建部份最近新刷了一层漆。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">7.shiny  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ ˈʃaɪni  ; NAmE ˈʃaɪni  /</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj.光亮的；锃亮的；反光的；有光泽的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英英释义：smooth and bright; reflecting the light</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">shiny black hair 有光泽的黑发</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">8.rug  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ rʌɡ  ; NAmE rʌɡ  /</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n.小地毯；垫子</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英英释义：a piece of thick material like a small carpet that is used for covering or decorating part of a floor</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">People put rugs on the ground. Rugs provide a soft place to walk.人们将地毯放在地上。地毯提供柔软的行走区。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">9.glitter  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ ˈɡlɪtə(r)  ; NAmE ˈɡlɪtər  /</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n.（装饰用的）小发光物</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英英释义：very small shiny pieces of thin metal or paper that are stuck to things as a decoration</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">gold/silver glitter 金色的╱银色的闪光装饰物</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">10.prop  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ prɒp  ; NAmE prɑːp  / </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n.道具</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英英释义：a small object used by actors during the performance of a play or in a film/movie</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He is responsible for all the stage props and lighting. 他负责全部舞台道具和灯光。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: I'</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">m</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;"> making some props for my next video project. It's going to be amazing!</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">那是闪光装饰物，我在为我的下一个视频项目做道具，效果会很棒！</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">A: But I can't wal</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">k a</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">cross the floor! I can</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">'t</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;"> even SEE the floor!</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">但是我没办法在地板上走了！我都看不见地板了！</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">B: I kn</span><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ow i</span></span></em><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;"> looks bad. Bu</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">, you know wha</span><span style="text-decoration: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;"> they say: You can</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">'t</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;"> ma</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ke a</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">n omelet withou</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;"> breaki</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ng a</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;"> few eggs!</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">我知道看起来很糟糕。但是，你知道：有失才有得！</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Digory now saw that where four trees grew close together their branches had all been laced together or tied together with switches so as to make a sort of cage. The two Elephants with their trunks and a few dwarfs with their little axes soon got it all undone. There were three things inside. One was a young tree that seemed to be made of gold; the second was a young tree that seemed to be made of silver; but the third was a miserable object in muddy clothes, sitting hunched up between them.    </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">迪格雷这才看见，四棵树紧紧地长在一起，树枝相互缠绕纠结，形成一个像笼子似的东西。两头大象用鼻子、几个小矮人用小斧很快分开了那些树枝。里面有三样东西：一棵小树，似乎是金子做的；另一棵像是银子做的小树；但第三样东西模样太惨，衣服上涂满泥浆，弓腰缩背地夹在两棵树之间。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：你收到来我聚会的邀请了吗?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：邀请函昨天到的邮箱。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：我担心它在邮寄过程中丢失了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：很遗憾，我不能参加你的聚会。我希望我可以去。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：很遗憾听到这个消息。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：我的岳母那天来。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：真的很遗憾那天你不能来。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：如果我能溜出家里，我会来的，但我的老婆会杀了我。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：我不想看到发生这样的事。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：你的下一个派对,我保证会去参加。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：如果你岳母再次拜访呢?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：值得庆幸的是,她一年只来一次。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Did you get the invitation to my party?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: The invitation came in the mail yesterday.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: I was worried it got lost in the mail.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Unfortunately, I can't go to your party. I wish I could.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: I'm sorry to hear that.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: My mother-in-law is visiting that day.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: I'm really sorry that you can't come.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: If I could sneak out of the house, I would, but my wife would kill me.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: I wouldn't want that on my hands.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: The next party you have, I promise I will be there.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: What if your mother-in-law visits again?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B; Thankfully, she only comes once a year.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">They ____________ the mountains and travelled to the valleys beyond.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他们越过群山，到了那边的山谷。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">crossed</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">汉译英</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">在全世界，有人做着意想不到的事：他们放慢节奏，而且发现 尽管习惯思维告诉你，假如你放慢节奏，就会被时代潮流抛弃，而事实上结果却相反。在合适的时候放慢节奏，人们发现他们做什么都做得更好。他们吃得更好，性生活更和谐，锻炼效果更好， 他们工作更棒，生活得也更好。而在这些时刻，这些地方，这些减速的行动中，就存在着许多人所说的国际慢活运动。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Right across the world, people are doing the unthinkable: they're slowing down, and finding that, although conventional wisdom tells you that if you slow down, you're road kill, the opposite turns out to be true: that by slowing down at the right moments, people find that they do everything better. They eat better; they make love better; they exercise better; they work better; they live better. And, in this kind of cauldron of moments and places and acts of deceleration, lie what a lot of people now refer to as the "International Slow Movement."</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><p style="text-align: center;outline: 0px;max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: 0.544px;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;"><strong style="outline: 0px;max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: 0.544px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="font-family:-apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, Helvetica Neue, PingFang SC, Hiragino Sans GB, Microsoft YaHei UI, Microsoft YaHei, Arial, sans-serif;">11.10 每日一句：</span></strong><strong style="outline: 0px;max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: 0.544px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="font-family:-apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, Helvetica Neue, PingFang SC, Hiragino Sans GB, Microsoft YaHei UI, Microsoft YaHei, Arial, sans-serif;">I'm working on it.    </span></strong></p><p style="text-align: center;outline: 0px;max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: 0.544px;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;"><strong style="outline: 0px;max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: 0.544px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;"><span style="font-family:-apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, Helvetica Neue, PingFang SC, Hiragino Sans GB, Microsoft YaHei UI, Microsoft YaHei, Arial, sans-serif;">我正努力做着呢/我正干着呢。</span></strong></p>
